Title: 

羅生門

----

Title-ruby: 

<ruby><rb>羅生門</rb><rt>らしょうもん</rt></ruby>

----

Title-english: Rashōmon

----

Author: 

<ruby><rb>芥川</rb><rt>あくたがわ</rt></ruby><ruby><rb>龍之介</rb><rt>りゅうのすけ</rt></ruby>

----

Author-english: Akutagawa Ryūnosuke

----

Blurb: Two down and out people meet under a gate in old Kyoto one evening, bringing both to examine the cost of survival.

Level: Advanced
